Once the players begin drawing tiles, they are typically placed on-edge before the players, so that each player can see his own domino tiles, but none can see the value of other players' tiles. Every player can thus see how many tiles remain in the other players' hands at all times during gameplay. One player begins by downing (playing the first tile) one of their tiles. In different games first tiles are also different. In Muggins player should start with the highest double (6-6), in Bergen the first move should be 0-0, in Mexican train each round starts with the next lower double. This tile starts the line of play, a series of tiles in which adjacent tiles touch with matching, i.e. equal, values. The players alternately extend the line of play with one tile at one of its two ends. The game ends when one player wins by playing their last tile, or when the game is blocked because neither player can play. If that occurs, whoever caused the block gets all of the remaining player points not counting their own.\r\n- Scoring game\r\nPlayers accrue points during game play for certain configurations, moves, or emptying one's hand. Most scoring games use variations of the draw game. In Muggins (All fives) player must make the open ends of the layout add up to 5s or a multiple of five (5s, 10, 15, 20, etc.) In bergen player scores when numbers on the open ends are equal. If a player does not call \"domino\" before the tile is laid on the table, and another player says 'domino' after the tile is laid, the first player must pick up an extra domino. In Mexican train the double zero domino is scored as 50 points.\r\n- Draw game\r\nIn a draw game (blocking or scoring), players are additionally allowed to draw as many tiles as desired from the stock before playing a tile. The score of a game is the number of pips in the losing player's hand plus the number of pips in the stock. Most rules prescribe that two tiles need to remain in the stock. The Draw game is often referred to as simply \"dominos\".\r\n\r\nIf you like board games like Checkers, Mahjong, Backgammon and Chess, you will love Dominoes: Best Classic Dominoes Board Game.","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9MT4VD18SCWZ","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"Cake Maker Master","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.11540.13815346590983924.b7da2166-32db-4103-a596-f50d5f99cd90.6adbadb6-290c-4d32-a64c-8e70e59cbea1","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"#464646","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.54179.13815346590983924.b7da2166-32db-4103-a596-f50d5f99cd90.290b67d6-9126-4252-9635-18d6d7b4d5e2","Height":300,"Width":620,"BackgroundColor":"#464646","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"නොමිලේ දෙන","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":5.0,"RatingsCount":"1","PackageFamilyNames":["35237JoyJourney.CakeMakerMaster_rqmgvvvsy2kse"],"ContentIds":["9bcc3b2b-e373-aee1-dce7-e3cfbcf494a1"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"  ","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC,HoloLens,ජංගම","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Welcome to My Cake Shop. විනාශ කිරීම, මිලිටරි හා ගුවන් යානා ගුවන් යානා දඩයම් කිරීම, ආයුධ සහ රට ආරක්ෂා කිරීම.\r\n\r\nඵෙතිහාසික යුද සටන්\r\n\r\nවාසනාවන්ත යුද ආඥාපති! ඔබ හමුදාවට නායකත්වය දෙනවා. මෙම යුධ උපාය මාර්ගයේ ඩ්රෝන් ක්රීඩාවෙහි සටන්කාමී ගුවන් හමුදා කඳවුරේ බලය ලබා ගැනීම සඳහා අවසන් ගුවන් ප්රහාරක ගුවන් භටයා වන්න. රොබෝට් වානේ ලෝකය හරහා සටන් කිරීම, හයි-ටෙක් යූ.ඒ.ඊ. ගුවන් ප්රහාරක රථ වාහන අණදීම සහ ඔබේ ඩ්රෝන් ප්රහාරයෙන් arsenal ගොඩනගා ගන්න. ඔබේ UCAV quadcopter ඩ්රෝන් ප්රහාරය වැඩිදියුණු කර මිසයිල හා මැෂින් තුවක්කු වලින් සන්නද්ධ කරන්න. බහු-ඉලක්කගත වෙඩි තැබීමේ මිසයිල පද්ධති සහ විශාල විනාශකාරී රොකට් එකතු කිරීම සහ
